Local News

Yesterday's Citizens' General Assembly

▲Estimated Attendance Over 100,000

▲Atmosphere Exceptionally Tense

The Shanghai Municipal Citizens' General Assembly for Suppressing Bandits, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese was held at 3:00 PM yesterday at the Nanshi Public Sports Ground. Over 100,000 citizens attended. The atmosphere throughout the venue was quite tense. The various aspects of yesterday's assembly are recorded below:

▲Participating Organizations: Yesterday's participants included the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Trade Associations of the Pharmaceutical, Medicinal Materials, Mercerized Cotton Weaving, Yarn, and Southern Goods Industries; the Labor Unions of the Publishing, Water and Electricity, Ink Manufacturing, Umbrella, Cigarette, Shipbuilding, Pharmaceutical, Cotton Spinning, Cotton Weaving, Sauce, Letterpress Printing, and Public Transportation Industries; the Farmers' Associations and Educational Associations of various districts; the various levels of Party Headquarters and branch offices; the Municipal Citizens' General Association, the National Goods Maintenance Association, the Chinese Liaison Society of the French Municipal Council, the Taxpayers' Association, and over 500 other organizations. Representatives included Wang Xiaolai, Zheng Chengqing, Hou Dachun, Wang Wenhua, Chen Peide, Lu Jingshi, Li Yongxiang, and Chen Yafu, totaling over 100,000 people.

▲Assembly Staff: Presidium: Wang Xiaolai, Wang Wenhua, Li Yongxiang, Zhu Xuefan, Gong Yuting, Zheng Chengqing, Hu Shuhua, Lin Kecong, Chen Yafu. Secretaries: Yan Esheng, Zhao Shusheng. General Commander of the City: Chen Peide. General Disciplinarian of the City: Zhou Xuexiang. General Commander of the Business Sector: Ye Jiaxing. Deputy Commander: Xie Zhongle. General Disciplinarian of the Business Sector: Ma Shaoquan. Deputy Disciplinarian: Shao Baoxing. General Commander of Zhabei: Wang Changyuan. Deputy Commander: Wang Yongliang. General Disciplinarian of Zhabei: Liu Xinquan. Deputy Disciplinarian: Tu Heyun. General Commander of Nanshi: Tang Junsheng. Deputy Commander: Long Peiyun. General Disciplinarian of Pudong: Ge Yunting. Deputy Disciplinarian: Zhang A'jin. Master of Ceremonies: Zhang Yaoming.

▲Assembly Procedure: (1) Play music; (2) Sing the Party anthem; (3) Entire assembly stand at attention; (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party, National flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (5) Observe a moment of silence; (6) The Chairman reverently reads the Last Will and Testament of Sun Yat-sen; (7) The Chairman delivers a speech; (8) Speeches; (9) Discussion of motions; (10) Shout slogans; (11) Play music; (12) Adjourn.

▲Chairman's Report: Chairman Wang Xiaolai reported, stating in brief: "Today, all Shanghai organizations have convened a general assembly for suppressing bandits, punishing rebels, opposing Japan, and aiding overseas Chinese. Since the scourge of the Red bandits has plagued our nation, numerous incidents have occurred, and internal and external troubles are constantly intensifying. The crisis is more severe than ever before. Unexpectedly, rebellious warlords have taken the opportunity to create chaos, remotely colluding with Japanese imperialism and the wicked Red bandits, disregarding the nation's survival and the people's welfare. All citizens of Shanghai should recognize that the Red bandits, warlords, and Japanese imperialism are the obstacles to our national revolution and the irreconcilable enemies of our 400 million compatriots. At this time of shared suffering, all our compatriots should pledge to eradicate evil thoroughly, spare no sacrifice in supporting the National Government, suppress the Red bandits, eliminate the rebels, safeguard the unity of the nation, and unite as one to back the opposition to Japan and aid to overseas Chinese. I hope that all fellow citizens in Shanghai and across the country will work hard."

▲Speeches from Various Sectors: Subsequently, Zhu Xuefan from the labor sector, Zheng Chengqing from the business sector, Chen Yafu from the agricultural sector, Zhang Honghai, a representative of Korean Overseas Chinese, and Li Yongxiang, a representative of the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association, delivered speeches. The long speeches are omitted.

▲Motions Passed: (1) That the Assembly send a telegram to General Commander Chiang Kai-shek and Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, as well as the frontline soldiers, to express our condolences and encourage them to strive to kill the enemy and complete the revolutionary task. Resolved: Unanimously passed. (2) That the Assembly send a circular telegram to military and civilian officials nationwide, calling for cooperation in the work of suppressing bandits and punishing rebels to quell internal unrest and resist foreign aggression. Resolved: Unanimously passed. (3) That the Assembly send a circular telegram to all organizations nationwide, calling for unified opposition to Japan and aid to overseas Chinese, and support for the National Government's suppression of bandits and punishment of rebels. Resolved: Unanimously passed. (4) That the anti-Japanese organizations in the city be established as permanent organizations. Resolved: Passed. (5) That a circular telegram be sent to all compatriots nationwide, urging them to uniformly consume domestic goods and reject Japanese goods. Resolved: Passed. (6) That the remaining funds from the previous Anti-Japanese National Salvation Fund be used as anti-Japanese and aid to overseas Chinese expenses. Resolved: Passed. (7) That labor education in the city be organized promptly. Resolved: Passed. (8) That the Municipal Government be petitioned to promptly forward a request to the Central Government for the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal General Labor Union and the Municipal Farmers' Association. Resolved: Passed. (9) That a declaration of the Assembly be issued. Resolved: Passed. (10) That all resolutions of the Assembly be entrusted to the Assembly Presidium to handle separately according to the established principles. Resolved: Passed. In addition, many other cases were passed, which are not listed here.

▲Declaration of the Assembly: The Assembly resolved to issue a declaration, which read: "For several years, the Chinese Communist Party, under the wings of red imperialists, has run rampant, especially in Hunan and Jiangxi provinces, which have suffered the most. In total, over 260,000 civilian lives have been lost, over 260,000 houses have been burned, and property losses are close to 100 million yuan. Moreover, in the areas affected by the Red scourge, all means of production have been destroyed, and even if the people are fortunate enough to escape slaughter, they cannot avoid being displaced, starving, and dying. We absolutely do not believe that this kind of inhuman brutality has any kind of doctrine as its goal, but is merely a return to the most barbaric and cruel banditry in history. Moreover, because it is subject to the influence of red

A Glimpse of the Citizens' Assembly (Photo by Our Newspaper)

To allow the avarice of color-obsessed imperialists to run rampant, mixed with bandits, is to certainly utterly destroy the people's livelihood, the society's existence, the nation's economy, the masses' lives, even to the point of national extinction and racial annihilation. Such a tragic outcome, anyone with even a little national thought and national consciousness, upon thinking of it, would not but gnash their teeth in hatred and vow not to coexist with the Red bandits in China. In May of this year, the National Assembly confirmed that the greatest disaster in China at present is the Red bandits, and unanimously resolved that suppressing the Red bandits is the most urgent task for the National Government and the people of the whole country. The government mobilized a large army, besieging and suppressing from all sides. Our frontline soldiers enduring the sweltering heat, traversing rugged terrain, bandaging wounds, and sacrificing their bodies to devote themselves to the work of suppressing bandits, is already obvious to everyone. Our Chairman of the National Government, Chiang Kai-shek, further entered Jiangxi to supervise the battle, vowing with life and death. In the past month, he has repeatedly captured important passes, and Ningdu and Donggu, the Red bandits' lairs, have also been successively captured. Thus, annihilating the mob and cutting off their roots is as easy as turning one's hand. At this point, our people nationwide should each do their duty, consistently assisting the government to complete the entire task of suppressing bandits. Unexpectedly, at this critical moment, Japanese imperialists, deliberately seeking trouble, instigated Koreans to massacre overseas Chinese, causing hundreds and thousands of casualties, and destroying countless properties, taking advantage of our government's focus on suppressing bandits, leaving it no time to attend to other matters, leading to a huge diplomatic dispute, in order to hold us hostage. The Wanbaoshan Incident, at most, was just a dispute caused by Korean farmers seizing land, which could be resolved by the Jilin Provincial Government and the Changchun County Government. However, Japanese ronin exaggerated the matter, spreading rumors and inciting trouble, determined to create an unprecedented tragedy for our Korean compatriots. And their frustrated warlords and politicians are even attacking the weakness and incompetence of their country's diplomacy, in order to force their government to become a second Tanaka Cabinet, sending troops to our country to obstruct the progress of bandit suppression. Our country, at this time, faces both internal strife and external aggression, pressing down on us simultaneously. How should the nation's soldiers follow the teachings of the Premier, obey the will of the people, and follow Commander-in-Chief Chiang, to engage in arduous and resolute struggle? Yet, Shi Yousan, with the wolfish ambition of a villain, stubbornly clinging to evil, levies funds and forcibly recruits soldiers, treating his defense area as private property, and viewing his subordinates as domestic slaves. As a member of the military, he disregards national laws, daring to raise troops in defiance of orders, plotting to disturb the peace of Tianjin and Beijing, endangering the party and the country, and willingly becoming a scapegoat for the enemy. Our central government, in the past, considering the people's hardship, has been lenient, comforting and tolerating, again and again. How could we have known that tolerating evil would only fuel the flames, and those who suffer would still be our people? In addition, the rebellious elements of Guangdong and Guangxi are watching Jiangxi and Hunan, supporting the Red bandits, acting as a screen. They have also secretly sent representatives such as Chen Youren to beg for pity from our eastern neighbor, currying favor with foreigners and selling out the country, which is known to all. Alas, how can our compatriots not be filled with anger? Reading Chairman Chiang's telegram from Nanchang on the 25th of this month, the rebellious elements in Guangdong are using 500,000 yuan to buy off Shi Yousan's troops, inciting rebellion, and secretly plotting to supply the Red bandits with guns and ammunition to prolong their existence. This further proves that the rebels inciting unrest, the warlords rebelling, the Red bandits rampaging, and the atrocities of Japanese imperialists, are all responding to each other, mutually causing each other. Without first pacifying the domestic situation, there is no way to resist foreign aggression. Alas, what has the party and the country done to wrong the rebels, that they must collude with warlords to create chaos, in order to prolong the life and ferocity of the Red bandits? If the people tolerate the warlords, then the warlords will surely further disrupt the unification and peace of the country. Therefore, the Red bandits must be suppressed, and the remnants of the warlords who created the opportunity for the Red bandits must especially be punished. Japan must be resisted, and the traitors and villains who collude with Japanese aggression must especially be annihilated. This is because these mad and unconscionable rebellious warlords, who cut themselves off from the people and alienate themselves from China, are no different from the Red bandits, no different from aliens. Our three million people of Shanghai, supporting the revolution, have been doing so for years. At this time of internal and external troubles, pressing down on us simultaneously, at this critical moment of life and death, after painful reflection, we know nothing else, but only know that the rebels who obstruct the suppression of bandits, the traitors who collude with age-old enemies, are all public enemies of our people and criminals of the country. We vow to support the central government, cleanse and sweep them away, and contribute money and efforts without hesitation. However, there is something that we especially cannot help but say. At this time of the new nation's founding, with hundreds of holes and thousands of wounds, to steady the situation and support what is in danger, we rely on leaders with a sense of responsibility. Our Chairman Chiang adheres to the teachings of the Premier, dedicates himself to the revolution, and takes suppressing bandits and punishing rebels as his own responsibility. He rushes to supervise the battle, being the vanguard of the people. Anyone with blood and qi cannot but be inspired. Furthermore, our generals, the pillars of the country, should especially clearly distinguish right from wrong, and differentiate obedience from disobedience. If they encourage their soldiers to eliminate traitors for the country, arrest Shi Yousan, and administer justice according to the law, so that there are no worries behind when suppressing bandits, and no concerns about traitors when dealing with foreign aggression, then they will have contributed to the country and will surely receive great rewards. If they willingly join the rebellion, refusing to turn back from the wrong path, then the will of the people and the law of the country will not tolerate them. Punishing and eradicating them will be the same as dealing with bandits, so that the seeds of rebellion will no longer remain, and unification and peace can be realized. As for our people nationwide, regarding the tragically deceased overseas Chinese, we should rescue the dying and heal the wounded, and avenge them. We especially wish to uphold the spirit of perseverance, make meticulous plans, and take deliberate actions, abiding by the rules of discipline, resolutely implementing economic severance with Japan, without the slightest compromise, in order to promote the awakening of the Japanese people and automatically stop the schemes of the stubborn warlords of that country. If there are those who are inherently disposed to currying favor with foreigners and are willing to sabotage, we must also uphold justice and abandon them with everyone. As long as we have a breath, this determination will not change. We humbly offer our sincerity and respectfully request your public consideration. Shanghai Municipal Citizens' Assembly for Suppressing Bandits, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese.

Declaration of the Assembly, July 30, Year 20.

Implementation of the Factory Law Starts Tomorrow

▲ Yan Zhuang Discusses Key Issues

The effective date of the Factory Law was originally scheduled to be the beginning of February this year.

Subsequently, after requests for postponement from various parties, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, considering the circumstances of industry and commerce, issued a notice postponing implementation for six months. Now, it has been determined that the effective date is from tomorrow (August 1st). Yesterday, Yan Zhuang, the Director of the Labor Department of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, came to Shanghai. This reporter inquired about the various circumstances regarding the implementation of the Factory Law. A summary of his conversation is recorded below: (1) Article 13 of the Factory Law, the issue of night work for female workers. The law clearly stipulates that female workers are not allowed to work from 10 PM to 6 AM the next morning. The intention of the law is to maintain morals and pay attention to the education of workers' children. The intention is good, but in reality, taking Shanghai as an example, there are at least 160,000 female workers in textile factories. If Article 13 of the law is implemented, at least 70,000 to 80,000 female workers will lose their jobs. What ability does the municipal government have to help them? And the immediate reduction in production is also an undeniable fact. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce has always taken promoting production and advocating worker welfare as its responsibilities in labor issues. Therefore, while maintaining the authority of the law, it also takes into account the dilapidated state of our country's industrial sector. Two weeks ago, it requested the Executive Yuan to find ways to provide relief. After discussion by the State Council, it was decided that "within two to three years, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce will urge factories to prepare for implementation." It was also submitted to the Central Political Conference for a decision. Yesterday, the Central Political Conference decided to postpone the implementation of that article for two years, with the Ministry of Industry and Commerce responsible for supervision. (2) Factory Law, one day off every seven days with pay. According to the regulations of the National Government, there are a total of eight legal holidays per year, all of which must be paid. If the Factory Law is followed, factories will have to pay for an additional 52 days of wages. In total, there will be two months of rest each year, which will have a significant impact on the production of our country's nascent industries. The significant losses to factories are secondary. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce, based on requests from various provinces and cities, and considering the circumstances, requested the Executive Yuan to find ways to remedy the situation. The State Council had already decided to submit it to the Judicial Yuan for interpretation. The 115th Standing Committee of the Central Government had already decided that the issue of paid holidays for workers should be handled in accordance with collective agreements and employment contracts. Therefore, the Judicial Yuan is requested to clarify whether the Central Government's decision during the period of political tutelage will remain effective after the implementation of the Factory Law. If the Judicial Yuan can understand the current actual situation of our country's immature industry, it will surely be able to find ways to remedy the situation later. (3) Factory conference, the qualification of factory representatives. In the factory conference, the factory and labor sides originally each had an equal number of representatives, from five to nine. However, according to the interpretation of the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce, only managers, deputy managers, factory directors, and deputy factory directors are qualified to represent the employer. If the factory follows the law, it will not be able to put forward five people as equal representatives for the factory conference. However, according to the interpretation of Article 6 of the Implementation Law of the Trade Union Law by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in a factory, in addition to managers, deputy managers, factory directors, and deputy factory directors, department heads, foremen, and even gatekeepers can represent the employer and exercise management rights. This is because the law clearly stipulates that "except for the factories listed in Article 3 of the Factory Law, all staff, employees, and workers may join trade unions, but those who represent the employer and exercise management rights are not included." The phrase "those who exercise management rights" naturally refers to the staff, employees, and workers in the previous sentence who are qualified to represent the employer. Therefore, those who cannot join trade unions can represent the employer and join the factory conference. This matter has also been discussed and decided by the Executive Yuan, and submitted to the Judicial Yuan for interpretation. It is expected that the Judicial Yuan will be able to provide satisfactory interpretations for the above two points within the next few days, so that our country's nascent industry will not be affected, and workers will not suffer job losses, while being able to obtain considerable protection and welfare.

Taking Over the French Courthouse Tomorrow Morning

▲ List of Judges Announced

After the agreement on the Shanghai French Concession Mixed Court was announced in Nanjing the day before yesterday, Mr. Gangarine, the French Consul General and negotiator for the French side, returned to Shanghai yesterday to rush the handover. Therefore, after the abolition of the courthouse, the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court and the Second Branch of the Shanghai Special District Local Court must be established on the date the agreement takes effect (i.e., August 1st). Current Status of Yangtze River Shipping

▲ Treacherous Merchants Smuggle Japanese Goods

▲ Changsha Gang Exclusively Loads Chinese Ships

▲ Treacherous Merchants Privately Transport Japanese Goods: Since various shipping companies implemented the ban on loading Japanese goods on the 24th, there is still a lot of Japanese fabric stored in this port, which cannot be transported to various ports along the Yangtze River. Recently, a certain merchant specializing in Japanese goods in Shanghai had a creative idea: entrusting the entire batch of Japanese cloth to a Japanese customs broker for declaration and loading on Japanese ships for export. Upon arrival at the destination, the goods are also picked up in the name of a Japanese merchant and then privately handed over to the treacherous merchant. In this way, the eyes and ears of the inspectors can be avoided. A certain amount of handling fee is given for each piece, and the Japanese are naturally happy to do so. Also, in view of the seizure of the cargo of the Lu Yang Gong in the barge the day before yesterday, from yesterday onwards, treacherous merchants transporting Japanese goods using barges have been inserting Japanese flags on the barges to indicate that they should not be inspected. As a result, the export volume of Japanese fabrics to the Yangtze River and the Northern and Southern Oceans is still quite high.

▲ Crowded Passengers and Goods in Changsha: Recently, Chinese merchant ships going upstream to Hankou have been very crowded with passengers and goods bound for Changsha from this port. There are two reasons for this: (1) Since the boycott, various passenger gangs in Hunan Province have refused to load on Japanese ships; (2) Last year, when the party was in Changsha, the godown of Jardine Matheson, a British company, was burned, and the passengers and goods were destroyed, amounting to nearly one million yuan. The passenger gangs demanded compensation from Jardine Matheson, but it was not approved. Therefore, various passenger gangs in Hunan Province have unanimously refused to transport on the company's merchant ships and are now exclusively loading on Chinese ships. Therefore, the Hunan-bound goods of China Merchants and Sanbei are very crowded.

▲ Goods No Longer Stored in Warehouses: This newspaper has reported twice that the floods in Hankou have submerged various warehouses. Although the water level is gradually receding, the water has not yet completely receded from the flooded warehouses, and various shipping companies are trying to move to higher ground. However, for the past few days, the various Jianglun ships of the Central American merchant have been unable to load large quantities of goods such as cane sugar and flour arriving in Hankou, because these goods would melt if they entered the water. Yesterday, various wheel bureaus discussed and decided that for the bureaus whose warehouses are submerged, when the ships arrive in Hankou, the goods will no longer be stored in the warehouses, and passengers will be notified to use barges for unloading, with the cost borne by the passengers. The original situation will be restored when the water recedes.

▲ Goods to Shanghai and Xun also Obstructed: Most of the goods from Shanghai to Jiujiang are transshipped to the interior and Nanchang, and vice versa. Yesterday, various ships in Shanghai received a telegram from Xun, saying that the Nanxun Road has been blocked by floods, and the transportation of goods in central Jiangxi has been obstructed. Furthermore, the warehouses cannot store goods, and the lighters have been fully loaded. Therefore, the import and export of passengers and goods have been obstructed.

Jardine Matheson Sailors Temporarily Accept Wage Cuts

The Shanghai Times reported that the issue of wage cuts between Jardine Matheson and its sailors has caused a tense situation for several weeks. The Chinese Coastal Western Sailors' Union held a meeting and decided that, in view of the current difficult business conditions, and for the sake of the overall situation, it would not force the company to accept the sailors' demands. The union sent a letter to the company yesterday, stating that it is willing to temporarily accept wages according to the current wage cut method. Therefore, the issue has been temporarily resolved.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Reiterates Penalties for Counterfeiting Trademarks

▲ Those Intending to Counterfeit Will Be Sentenced to Two Years in Prison and Fined 3,000 Yuan

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce received instructions from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday, It is hereby ordered to comply, It has been learned that those who intend to deceive others by counterfeiting registered or unregistered trademarks shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than two years and fined not more than 3,000 yuan, Article 268 of the Criminal Law has clearly stipulated, And counterfeiting the registered trademark of others can be regarded as counterfeiting, which has also been interpreted by the Legislative Yuan, Therefore, whether counterfeiting or imitating the registered trademark of others is strictly prohibited by law, However, it has been found that some unscrupulous merchants recently deliberately distort the provisions of the law, arguing that there are no special articles in the law for punishment, and dare to imitate the registered trademarks of others with the intention of making profits, This is a violation of the rights of others and should be reiterated so that they know that imitating the registered trademarks of others should be considered counterfeiting, If such imitation of the registered trademark of others occurs again in the future, the government will, for the sake of protecting the exclusive right to use the trademark, enforce the law and not lightly attempt to do so, lest they fall into the trap of the law, In addition to ordering, it is hereby ordered that the association inform the merchants, etc., to comply with the requirements, This order,

Various Trade Associations Oppose Jiangsu Province's Request for Assistance with Business Tax

▲ Telegraphed the Executive Yuan to Order a Cease

(Guómín News Agency) Yesterday, over a hundred trade associations, including the silk and satin industry, mercerized cotton weaving industry, and dried goods industry in this city, telegraphed the Executive Yuan to order a halt to the Jiangsu Provincial Government's request for assistance with business tax funds from this city. The telegram reads: "Respectfully to the esteemed Executive Yuan of the Nanjing National Government, we have learned that the business tax is intended to offset the losses from the abolition of líjīn (internal tariffs) at the local level. This city has never had líjīn revenue and originally did not need to consider this. However, in order to assist in the city's administration and to implement the Premier's Grand Shanghai Plan, even in a time of commercial decline, the citizens are willing to contribute to fulfill their civic duties. Unexpectedly, the Jiangsu Provincial Government has made a move to request assistance with business tax funds from the authorities of this city, which violates the original intention of the citizens' tax payment. Moreover, the business tax is a local tax and should be used for local undertakings. If it is used for businesses outside the locality, it also goes against the original intention of the tax system. Therefore, we dare to appeal to your esteemed Yuan to order a halt to this. Otherwise, it is not what the citizens of this city would willingly accept. We are telegraphing in trepidation and await your orders."

The Domestic Goods Market Will Seek a New Location

▲ Yesterday, a Special Representative Meeting Was Held and Resolved

The Domestic Goods Market has been forced to close for nearly two months. The Shanghai Municipal Government has ordered the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce to investigate and report all losses suffered by various manufacturers and the market as a whole, in order to negotiate with the Municipal Council (of the Shanghai International Settlement). Yesterday, all the manufacturers held a special representative meeting for this matter. More than sixty people attended, including Liu Zhongying, Zhou Zhaolin, Hu Shengyao, Tang Rongqin, etc. Liu Zhongying was elected as chairman. The resolutions were: (1) To submit a petition to the Municipal Government, detailing the manufacturers' plight and requesting that negotiations with the Municipal Council be expedited. (2) To send a letter to the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, requesting that personnel be dispatched as soon as possible to investigate the extent of the losses. (3) At this critical time of intense boycott of Japanese goods, domestic goods manufacturers should rise up together to fulfill the original purpose of saving the country through domestic goods. Now that the market has been sealed for no reason, the question of how to find another way out was discussed. It was resolved that, in addition to petitioning the Municipal Government to expedite negotiations with the Municipal Council, a suitable location should be sought to open a market, so as to fulfill the principle of exchanging goods for goods. (4) To send a letter to the Citizens' Society for the Promotion of Domestic Goods, requesting the initiation of a mobile exhibition of domestic goods, so that compatriots in various regions have the opportunity to recognize domestic goods. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Request to Form a Maritime Court to Adjudicate the "Dà Chāng" Ship Sinking Case

After the Dà Huá Company's Dà Chāng ship was sunk by the Pingan Company's Dà Huá ship, an agreement was made for public arbitration. After lengthy negotiations, it has not yet been realized. Now, the Dà Huá Company has decided to request the Ministry of the Navy to form a maritime court to publicly adjudicate the case, to clarify responsibility and expedite the decision. The following is what has been heard:

Dispute Over Arbitration Contract Dà Huá and Pingan each sent personnel to the Navigation Association to sign an arbitration contract for this case. Dà Huá argued that the arbitrators should be one appointed by each side, and another jointly appointed by the two arbitrators. This would allow for mutual arbitration, and if they disagree, the final judgment could be made solely by the third party, which would be fairer. However, Pingan did not agree very much, arguing that only one person should be used. Dà Huá rejected this, saying that having one person arbitrate would lead to many abuses and there would be no remedy.

▲ Unable to Agree on a Settlement Dà Huá put forward the reasons why three arbitrators would be the most appropriate, but could not obtain Pingan's approval. Yu Qiaqing of the Shanghai Navigation Association believed that because both sides were holding their ground, the case was being prolonged. Now that Dà Huá was suffering a significant loss alone, it was indeed something Pingan would be happy to see, which was not fair. Therefore, he proposed mediation to both sides, changing to a subsidized settlement, which would resolve the matter quickly. However, this method was not desired by the China United Assurance Corporation and Dà Huá, and thus could not proceed.

▲ Petitioned the Ministry of the Navy for Public Adjudication Dà Huá Company believes that the sinking of the Dà Chāng resulted in losses of hundreds of thousands of yuan. This matter has not yet been compensated by Pingan, and arbitration is unable to proceed. Now, the company has decided to submit the case to the Ministry of the Navy, requesting the Ministry to form a maritime court to hear the case and determine responsibility, so that the victims can receive compensation. Yesterday, Mr. Qin of the company told reporters that the petition was being prepared.

▲ Unpaid Customs Fees The Jianghai Customs spent 77,000 taels to blow up the Dà Chāng, which must be acknowledged by the shipowner. Currently, the Shanghai shipping community is working hard to request an amendment to the maritime law, stating that the cost of salvaging sunken ships by customs should not be borne by the shipowner. Yesterday, the Ministry of Communications issued an order stating that it had asked the Executive Yuan to consult with the Legislative Yuan to amend this article. Therefore, Dà Huá has not yet paid the blasting fee. In recent days, the iron plates of the blasted Dà Chāng ship have been salvaged and auctioned off by customs workers.

The new Heng Zi Money Exchange has been established in Qingshun Li, Beijing Road, with a capital of 30,000 taels. The shareholders are Wang Ziting, Yao Yinzu, Yu Jinfu, Zhu Xinru, Xie Jinyuan, etc. The manager is Wu Zhengyun. The Rooftop Garden of the New World Hotel

The New World Hotel on Nanjing Road, at the Mud City Bridge, is the most perfect hotel in Shanghai. The size of its halls is the largest among the major hotels in Shanghai, the layout is exquisite, the decorations are elegant and clean, and the rent is low, which is beyond the reach of other hotels. Recently, the interior has been greatly renovated, and the room arrangements are exceptionally beautiful. The top floor has recently been opened as a rooftop garden. For the convenience of the guests, Chinese and Western cuisine and ice rooms have been added. Moreover, the location of the hotel is adjacent to the racecourse, and the air is fresh and beneficial to health. The weather has been extremely hot and stuffy in recent days, and one feels refreshed and energized upon reaching the rooftop of the hotel, and there are various cold foods to relieve the heat, making it truly a good place to escape the summer heat.

"The Secrets of the Arctic" Premieres in Paris Today

In 1928, the Italian explorer Nobile was in danger in the Arctic. The Russian government specially organized a rescue team to search for traces, which took several months and cost millions. Finally, Nobile and some of the people were rescued in the Arctic, but the whereabouts of Amundsen and others who went with Nobile are unknown and were unable to return safely. Recently, Nobile heard that it was rumored in Moscow that Amundsen was still alive in the Arctic, so he once again led explorers from various countries on the Russian icebreaker Maligin on the 18th of this month to explore the Arctic. The film "The Secrets of the Arctic," which is premiering at the Paris Grand Theater today, is a true depiction of the tragic exploration history of 1928. From beginning to end, it was filmed on location. Everything in the film is of special interest. Watching it is not only entertaining, but also increases knowledge.

Several comrades from the business community are using their spare time to study the art of Peking Opera. They have specially organized an opera club, named the United Arts Society. The inauguration ceremony and welcoming ceremony for the vice president will be held at 2:00 PM tomorrow. It is believed that the club's future development will be flourishing.

Representatives' Meeting of the National Goods Factory Alliance

The Shanghai National Goods Factory Alliance held a meeting of member representatives yesterday, and the results of the discussion were: (1) Regarding the case of whether, in the event that various members encounter raw materials and necessities that cannot be replaced, they should apply to the Anti-Japanese Association after obtaining certification from a domestic goods organization when purchasing, it was resolved that each factory should report the raw materials to the Alliance for registration and application, and then forward them to the Anti-Japanese Association. Therefore, an Industrial Raw Materials Review Committee was organized, and Tianyiwei Mother Factory, Wuzhou Pharmacy, Samsung Cotton Iron Factory, Dà China Welfare Rubber Factory, China Enamel Factory, Jisheng Industrial Society, and Scientific Instrument Museum were appointed as reviewers on the spot. (2) It was proposed that the trademarks of members' products be compiled into a booklet and distributed to various agencies, groups, and anti-Japanese associations across the country for record-keeping, in order to avoid misunderstandings. It was resolved to do so. (3) Before the Domestic Goods Guide is printed, anti-Japanese associations across the country will be notified that if they encounter goods that cannot be identified, they can write to the Alliance to inquire and avoid wrongful detention. It was resolved to do so. (4, 5, 6) Omitted in brief.

The Sales of Sheng Dan are Booming

The Sheng Dan, a domestic product produced by the Jiu Fu Company, has an established reputation as an essential health product for the summer. This time, the Xie Xing Pharmaceutical Factory, in the midst of the anti-Japanese and overseas Chinese support movement, spared no expense in promoting it on a large scale, and prepared many samples for free distribution, hoping that those who have always blindly believed in imported Dan can take this opportunity to recognize the fragrance and efficacy of domestic Sheng Dan, and unanimously promote it. In the early stages, advertisements for guessing games were published in various newspapers and periodicals to test the extent to which people from all walks of life knew about this Sheng Dan. As a result, more than 48,000 letters were received, of which less than 2,000 were mistakenly guessed as Ballantine's or other products. This shows that all sectors have a unified understanding of the domestic Sheng Dan, and that its low price, color, fragrance, and superiority to imported Dan are especially in the minds of all sectors. This can be said to be a great success in terms of domestic goods. It is now heard that the Xie Xing Pharmaceutical Factory expresses its deep gratitude for this, and all those who guessed correctly will be given a small package of Sheng Dan, and those who did not guess correctly will also be given a sample, as a small token of appreciation. They are now being sent out by hand, and the sales of Sheng Dan are also in a state of being unable to meet the demand, and work is being stepped up.

Local News Two

Shuài Sòngpíng's Sentencing Date

▲ August 4th

Shuài Sòngpíng, a Jiangxi native who has held prominent official positions in the past, engaged in kidnapping after leaving the political arena. The kidnapping of Lu Shaotang, the compradore of the Fair Price Foreign Firm, last year was instigated by Shuài. He was apprehended by Chief Inspector Lu Liankui of the General Inspectorate and handed over to the Special District Court. The various circumstances of the interrogation have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Xu Jiashi, the presiding judge of the criminal division of the Special Court, held another hearing in the first criminal court. He first briefly questioned Shuài Sòngpíng. Shuài completely denied the kidnapping of Lu and hired lawyer E Sen to defend him. The court then ordered the debate to begin. The police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated that after solving the case, the police found that the gang's headquarters was in the Great East Hotel, and the place where the hostage was held was in a house owned by Cheng Zhongshi on Hart Road. When Shuài was arrested, the waiter at the Great East Hotel identified the defendant as going to the gang's headquarters, and Cheng Zhongshi's accountant also identified the defendant as the person who came to rent the house, who at the time claimed to be named Wang Zhishan. Moreover, the criminal who had already been sentenced provided evidence. The defendant claimed that he was not in Shanghai at the time of the incident, but the letters found by the police at his home were all sent to the defendant at the time of the incident. Therefore, the evidence in this case is unusually sufficient, and he should be severely punished according to the law. However, lawyer E Sen argued that the waiter at the Great East Hotel and the criminals who rented the house on Hart Road all said that the Shuài Sòngpíng they had seen before was fatter than the defendant. According to the precedents of the Supreme Court, vague confessions cannot be considered positive evidence. The police submitted letters proving that the defendant was in Shanghai, which was incorrect, because Shuài's departure from Shanghai was not announced to friends and relatives beforehand, so friends and relatives only knew that he was in Shanghai, so the letters were sent to him, not knowing that he had already left Shanghai. This point is also insufficient to prove guilt, and he should be declared innocent. Judge Xu then announced that the debate was over and scheduled the sentencing for the morning of August 4th.

Two Kidnappers Executed by Firing Squad

▲ Four Kidnapping Cases

▲ One Major Robbery Case

The Chinese and Western detectives of the Hongkou Police Station previously arrested Shi Jinde, a 23-year-old native of Suzhou, and Li Wenbing, a 21-year-old local (native of Tongzhou), on suspicion of kidnapping. Investigations revealed that on November 4, 1929, they kidnapped Lou Kenzai, a student at the Qianye Public School on Peng Road. On December 6 of the same year, they kidnapped Xi Lusheng, the compradore of HSBC, in front of the Yizhi Xiang restaurant on Fuzhou Road, and shot him dead on the spot. On February 19, 1930, they kidnapped Zhang Zukang, the Soy Sauce King, on Wuchang Road. On April 14, they kidnapped Zhang Xinglian and Zhang Hualian, sons of Zhang Shouchong, the Director of the Department of Finance, on Daxi Road, extorting huge sums of money. They were also major criminals in the robbery of 46,000 yuan from the Four Banks Reserve Treasury on the Bund of Fuzhou Road on March 13. They were handed over to the Special District Court for interrogation and were sentenced to death in various places. After being approved by the superiors, the execution date arrived yesterday morning. At 8:30 AM, the police escorted the two criminals, Shi and Li, to the Third Criminal Court of the Special Court, where Judge Cheng Shangfeng presided. He asked the two criminals if they had any last words and to write letters to their families. Shi Jinde confessed, "Please notify Mrs. Xue at No. 21 Taichang Li, Dong Youheng Road, to come and collect the body. I have nothing else to say." Li Wenbing confessed, "Please consult the slaughterhouse on the opposite side of the Changjiang Road in the French Concession, next to Tongkang Li, which is my home. Today is the execution date, so there is no need for anyone to collect the body. However, my family is very poor, and I have not received a penny of the kidnapped money." The attitudes of the two criminals, Shi and Li, were strong and fearless, and they were rude to the detectives in charge of the case. Judge Cheng stopped them in court and ordered the Chinese and Western police to take Shi and Li down, put them in a car along with the files and photos, and drive to the Caohejing Second Prison execution ground. Yang, a prosecutor from the Local Court, was appointed as the supervising officer. He ordered Police Chief Xu Jinqing, Police Inspector Chen Xihui, and execution police officers Wang Jianqing, Xu Guoguang, Yin Daoxu, Zhang Chunsen, etc., to rush to the Caohejing Second Prison execution ground. After the judge and Warden Dong took their seats, they examined the prisoners one by one. The judge then ordered the execution, and Chief Xu directed the execution police to take them down and execute them by firing squad. The bodies were collected and sealed by the hall.

Gang Fight Among Workers from Hubei at Hongsheng Wharf

▲ Xiexing Gong and Anlu Inn

▲ Dispute Arising from Competition for Business

▲ Anlu Inn Suffers Defeat

Several hundred workers from Hubei Province engaged in a gang fight at Hongsheng Wharf in Pudong's Lannidu the night before last, due to a dispute over the proper order of unloading cargo from ships. As a result, many sustained knife wounds of varying severity. The details of the investigation are recorded below:

▲ Both Groups of Workers Have Their Reasons: The incident originated on the 24th of this month, when workers from the Hubei gang, including Li Gaoyu, Liu Hanxiang, Zhong Daokai, and others, jointly submitted a petition to the Third District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. It stated that they were representatives of the Xiexing Gong 131 Workers' Group, engaged in the business of transporting goods to and from the Taikoo Company and Hongsheng Wharf for many years. Recently, Jiang Yushan and Gao Hanqing, representatives of Taikoo Anlu Inn, had incited laborers to seize their business, and they requested police protection. While the police were investigating, Jiang Yushan and others from Anlu Inn also submitted a petition to the Third District, requesting registration. Their petition stated that there were hundreds of fellow villagers residing under their jurisdiction who relied on working at the wharves for their livelihood. Due to the large number of people, disputes often arose. After discussions among the villagers, it was decided that all customs-declared goods going to and from the Taikoo Company and Hongsheng Wharf would be handled by Xiexing Gong workers. The scattered miscellaneous goods outside the ship that did not need to enter the warehouse would be transported by Anlu Inn workers. This arrangement had been in place for over ten years without any problems. Now, Li Gaoyu and others from Xiexing Gong were relying on their large numbers to forcibly occupy all the miscellaneous goods that did not need to enter the warehouse, which was bound to cause trouble.

▲ Dispute Arises, Mediation Fails: District Chief Zhang, seeing that both sides had their own arguments, feared that these people would riot. He sent several experienced police officers to the wharf every day to suppress any disturbances. The day before yesterday afternoon, when a Wanjia steamer arrived at Hongsheng Wharf, the Xiexing Gong workers continued to unload the customs-declared goods as usual. However, both sides held onto the miscellaneous goods outside the ship, refusing to yield, and each gathered many people to wait at the wharf. District Chief Zhang of the Third District, believing that these people were about to resort to violence, dispatched a platoon of armed police officers to the scene. At the same time, he summoned the representatives of both sides, Li Gaoyu and Jiang Dashan, for questioning, instructing them to continue their respective businesses according to the old customs. However, Li Gaoyu and others from Xiexing Gong firmly refused. Then, Chief Chang Caichen was called in to mediate, urging both sides to compromise. While Anlu Inn had already expressed their willingness to compromise, Xiexing Gong still insisted on their previous demands, causing Chang to resign from his mediation duties without any result. It was already six o'clock in the evening.

▲ Gang Fight Results in Injuries: District Chief Zhang, seeing that the ship had been delayed for too long and was obstructing traffic, instructed the representatives of both sides to send half of their workers to unload the cargo, with each side receiving half of the wages. He told them to return to the district the next morning (i.e., yesterday) at eight o'clock to await mediation. If mediation failed, they would be transferred to the court for investigation. However, not long after the representatives left, the workers on both sides suddenly clashed. The scene became chaotic, with shouts and police whistles filling the air. The number of police officers at the scene was insufficient to stop the fight. As a result of the gang fight, Anlu Inn was outnumbered and two people were stabbed: (1) Jiang Hanrong, three knife wounds to the arm; (2) Gao Chunlin, three knife wounds to the leg. On the Xiexing Gong side, Zhang Yuming and Zhong Daokai were injured, but not seriously. Subsequently, the water patrol team arrested Li Gaoyu, Xiang Yuren, and Wang Wenan, three people involved in the incident.

▲ Xiexing Gong Representative Handed Over to the General Bureau: After Jiang Hanrong and others were injured, they were bleeding profusely and unable to move. Fellow workers carried them to the Third District, where the district chief immediately sent all the police officers to arrest the culprits. However, they had already scattered and fled. The injured were then transferred to the nearby Pudong Hospital for treatment. That evening, the doctors examined them one by one and bandaged their wounds. Yesterday morning at eight o'clock, they were brought back and handed over to the local court for investigation. The Xiexing Gong representative, Li Gaoyu, was transferred by the water patrol team to the Public Security General Bureau for disposition.

Zou Aizhen Withdraws Lawsuit Against Dr. Tang

▲ Tang Already Involved in Litigation at the Special Court

▲ Zou Disregards Transfer for Trial

Zou Aizhen, the wife of economic doctor Tang Chongci (i.e., Tang Huixuan), filed a lawsuit in the local court, accusing him of abandonment and seeking a divorce. The court had summoned Tang Chongci, but he did not appear, and the court ordered a further summons, as reported in previous news. Yesterday, the continued hearing was held again. At ten o'clock in the morning, Zou Aizhen, accompanied by lawyer Yang Zhihao, arrived at the court to await the hearing. Soon after, Judge Tong Shenglü specially opened the Eighth Tribunal. The defendant, Tang Chongci, did not appear. The official summoned Zou Aizhen to the case and said, "According to the bailiff's report, Tang Chongci currently resides in the Public Concession, 48 Baoshan Lane, Baoding Road. However, personnel cases are subject to special trial. According to the Civil Procedure Law, this court will transfer the case to the Special Court for trial." Lawyer Yang replied, "After the plaintiff applied to your court for mediation on May 8, the defendant initiated litigation in the Special Court, which is clearly an evasion. I request public service." The official said, "If the defendant's address is unknown, public service may be allowed. However, since the defendant has a definite address, the procedure is improper, and the request cannot be granted." Zou Aizhen then stated, "I request the presiding judge to transfer jurisdiction to the Special District Court for your court to try. Moreover, the defendant suddenly filed a lawsuit in the Special Court, intending to deceive the authorities, which is quite obvious. I speculate that the Special Court may not be clear about everything that happened between us." The official said, "You have been involved in litigation for a long time, and the newspapers have reported in detail. It is expected that the Special Court will have a clear understanding early on. If you do not want to transfer the case to the Special Court, you might as well withdraw the lawsuit." Lawyer Yang replied, "I request to withdraw." The official ordered her to sign and leave the court.

Judgment in the Case of an Indian Guard Committing Assault

▲ Warning to All Gatekeepers and Police

▲ Use of Force Must Be More Careful

The "Great American Evening News" reported that this morning (30th), British police magistrate Haines, when hearing the case of Indian man Meng Shaxin assaulting a rickshaw puller, warned all gatekeepers and Indian police officers not to abuse force when performing their duties. Meng Shaxin was the night shift Indian guard at He Dong's residence at 157 Seymour Road. Yesterday (29th) afternoon, he used a staff to violently beat rickshaw puller Qi Hexin, causing serious injuries and breaking Qi's left pinky finger. This morning, he was brought to the British police court for interrogation. The rickshaw puller testified that he was beaten for parking his rickshaw in front of He Dong's residence to eat. Mrs. Kerkes, a Western woman who witnessed the incident, and Mr. Hulf, the Western rickshaw owner, also testified in court. The magistrate sentenced Meng Shaxin to 21 days of imprisonment with hard labor, and declared that there had been frequent incidents of Indians assaulting Chinese people this month. This kind of abuse of force must be stopped immediately. Therefore, all gatekeepers and Indian police officers are warned to be more careful when using force.

Another Person Involved in the Case of a Westerner Purchasing Arms

▲ Zhenjiang Native Wei Xiaolan

Russian Bi Ke Leweisigai, for impersonating a National Government military officer to order a huge amount of arms from Lai Fa Foreign Firm using counterfeit documents, was detained by the patrol room to the Special District Court for interrogation. This has been reported in this newspaper before. It is now known that the chief detective Ma Wenda of the General Patrol Room and the Western detective Beibeining have found that Wei Xiaolan from Zhenjiang is also suspected of being involved in this case. They arrested Wei at 33 Mingde Lane, Pushi Road in the French Concession at 9:30 on the morning of the day before yesterday and brought him to the patrol room. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Criminal Division One of the Special District Court, where Judge Xu Jiashi presided over the interrogation. The patrol room's lawyer, Ru Bao Yi, stated that the patrol room requested to temporarily detain Wei Xiaolan because Wei also went to the plaintiff Lai Fa's office when Leweisigai went there, saying that he was the secretary of Zhang Faying, a representative of the National Government. However, the patrol room has not yet determined whether Wei will be a defendant or a witness. Lai Fa then testified that Wei Xiaolan had come to his office twice. The first time was on May 24th, when he came with Leweisigai. According to Leweisigai, Wei was Zhang Faying's secretary, but he did not speak English. Wei Xiaolan stated that he did not know Leweisigai, but was introduced by a Russian named Xue Ge Lai, who said that there was a transaction with a Chinese businessman and asked him to act as an interpreter. Xue was a colleague of the former Jinpu Railway. He then went to Leweisigai's residence at 24 Shengmuyuan Road. Leweisigai then took him to Lai Fa's office. What they discussed was all about arms. He did not want to object at the time, so he tolerated it. After he left, he negotiated with Leweisigai, and Leweisigai said, "Why are you so timid?" Later, Leweisigai came again, asking him to go to the plaintiff's office again. He refused and advised him not to do such a dangerous thing. Leweisigai then said to him, "You are so timid, so you cannot be called a military commander, but only a secretary." He insisted that he go with him, so he had no choice but to go. He heard Leweisigai say to Lai Fa, "You must find a Chinese person to be a guarantor." Lai Fa said to Leweisigai, "The draft contract can be given to you tomorrow." After he left, he asked Leweisigai what he meant. Leweisigai said that they wanted a Chinese person to be a guarantor, and after he signed the contract, they would entrust a lawyer to ask him for money. If he refused, they would report to the National Government and would achieve the purpose of defrauding money. After Bik Leweisigai was arrested, the newspapers all reported on the matter. Then, an old Russian named Xue Ge Lao came to ask him if he had stopped the matter because of this. He answered yes and then asked him who would go after he left. Xue claimed to be the person who packed opium for him. After the patrol room arrested him, they went to arrest the individual Xue mentioned, but he had disappeared. He graduated from St. Francis School and has served in the Wah Nan and Peace Foreign Firms, so he is familiar with most of the foreign firms. This time, he was really implicated. Judge Xu then ordered him to be detained and interrogated again at a later date.

Robbery on Qiale Road

The Wang family, who run a hardware business at 3 Changxing Lane, Qiale Road, Nanyang Bridge in the French Concession, were suddenly visited by three robbers at 9:30 yesterday morning. Two of the robbers were wearing silk long gowns, and one was wearing a short jacket, speaking with local accents. Each held a pistol and broke in through the front door. The house was a double-wing building, and the Wang family lived alone. The robbers shouted to silence them and drove the Wang family mistress and servants into a room. One robber guarded the door and began ransacking boxes and cabinets at will. After searching, they found the owner's bank checks and deposit books. The robbers ordered the Wang family owner to sign a check for 1,000 yuan payable immediately, to withdraw foreign currency. The remaining robbers waited in the room. From morning to about 1 pm, the robbers who went to withdraw the money did not return. The owner and his wife wanted to urinate, so they begged the robbers for convenience. The robbers allowed the Wang family mistress to go to another room to relieve herself. Unexpectedly, the Wang family was alert and closed the door, shouting for help. The robbers, seeing that the matter had been exposed, immediately fled with the loot. The Wang family's rickshaw puller was indeed a brave man and followed the robbers, shouting loudly to catch them. Finally, one robber was captured. The strangest thing was that when the robbers were being arrested, a white-牌 taxi drove up, apparently hired by the robbers for escape. The detectives detained them all at the Songshan Road patrol room. It is reported that there were a total of five robbers, three entering the house and two guarding outside. It was then learned by the patrol room that the robbers gathered and departed from room 414 of the Shenzhou Hotel. The remaining robbers are currently being searched for and the original stolen goods are being recovered.

Letter from Wine Merchants to the Director of the License Tax Bureau

Hua Dong News reported that the Zhabei Yuanyuanheng and other wine merchants sent a letter to Gu Daosheng, the director of the Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau, saying: "Director Gu Daosheng, Greetings. We hereby inform you that our company sent a representative to exchange licenses and pay taxes the day before yesterday. We learned that your bureau has changed the grades of the old licenses from the previous session and increased the taxes. For example, the old Yuanyu Company has always been a Class B license, which should pay 4 yuan. Now it has been changed to Class A, adding 4 yuan. Most of the households, such as Guangda, have always been Class C, and should pay 2 yuan each, but now they have been changed to Class B, adding 2 yuan. This kind of tax increase policy was not notified in advance and was suddenly increased when people were unprepared. According to the tax administrative procedures, the burden on merchants may be excessive. However, the Yuanyu and other companies belong to merchants, and although they feel the pain of this unilateral high pressure for this heavy tax that was levied without notice, they have no choice but to try their best to pay, since it is related to the country's economy. Unexpectedly, in addition to this sudden tax increase, two corners were added to the mother tax of one yuan. Since the collection fee is noted to be exempt, this additional 20% has not been noted on the license under which item, nor has it been announced to the taxpayers what it is for. Such tax collection is increased, and then collected again, with layers of squeezing, not only can the business power not support it, but also adds a kind of unfounded extra burden. As far as doubts are concerned, we are sending a letter for your reference, hoping that your bureau will understand and clearly show us what to follow."

Recent News on Road Administration in the Public Concession

▲ Expenses for Purchasing Land and Releasing Roads in the Central District

▲ Propose Temporarily Postponing Organization Within This Year

The Public Concession Bureau released the minutes of the Public Works Committee meeting on the 21st of this month. According to the report of the Accounting Office, the expenses for widening and expanding roads in the first half of this year have reached 1,095,902 taels, which is only 704,094 yuan according to the budget. At present, the Bureau's expenditures on investment are huge, and it is difficult to allocate more funds. It is proposed to temporarily postpone the implementation of road improvement projects that are not urgent. According to the director of the Engineering Department, most of these expenses are due to the purchase of land and the widening of roads when houses are rebuilt in the central district. Land prices in the central district are higher, and the cost is inevitably higher. However, if the opportunity to purchase land is taken, the realization of the Bureau's road improvement plan will be delayed for many years. After discussion by the committee members, it was proposed to temporarily postpone the implementation of projects that are not of major importance this year, but it is also necessary to consider the situation of citizens rebuilding houses and handle them appropriately.

Continued News on the Reorganization of the Guangdong Businessmen's Hospital

The Guangdong Businessmen's Hospital, founded by the Guangdong overseas Chinese in Shanghai, had been reorganized by the directors due to the proposal of Dr. Chen Daming, who expressed his sympathy. Recently, Dr. Huang Wen and nine others have been hired to take charge of medical affairs. It is said that Dr. Huang and others are scheduled to take over everything at the hospital from tomorrow (August 1st). Dr. Chen Daming is very busy with medical affairs and has not been involved in the hospital's medical affairs. It is reported that Dr. Chen is also working at the hospital, which is a false rumor.

Traffic to Mogan Mountain Has Resumed

▲ China Travel Service Continues to Sell Joint Tickets

The China Travel Service in this city previously suspended the sale of joint transportation tickets from Shanghai to Mogan Mountain due to heavy rain in Hangzhou and floods in Wukang Mountain, which caused the traffic from Hangzhou to Mogan Mountain to be severely flooded and impassable for cars. It is now reported that the weather has cleared since the day before yesterday, the water has receded, and traffic has resumed. Cars can directly reach the foot of the mountain, so the company has resumed selling joint transportation tickets to the mountain as usual.

Liang Saizhen Sues "Camera" Tabloid

The "Camera" tabloid at 12 Pike Road published a section of "Unofficial History of the Silver Screen" in its June 20th issue, which included a passage about Liang Saizhen's abandoned child, stating that Liang had a relationship with Xu Qinfu, a colleague at the Star Film Company, and did not take care of the child she bore, causing him to be dirty and resembling a beggar. During mealtimes, she did not allow him to sit down, so the child secretly scooped up cat food to fill his hunger, resulting in cat fish scales sticking to his mouth, a pitiful sight that was difficult to describe. After reading the report, Liang Saizhen, believing that she had been able to gain audience favor for the films she starred in at the Star Film Company because of her reputation and artistry, filed a criminal self-suit against the editor and author of "Camera" with the Special District Court through lawyer Zhan Jifeng, requesting that they be punished in accordance with Article 325 of the Criminal Law for damaging her reputation and ruining her credibility. Yesterday morning, Judge Ge Zhitan of the Special Court opened a court session to summon them. The "Camera" tabloid was represented by editor Zhang Yuyan, accompanied by lawyer Da Yaoxian, to respond to the suit. Lawyer Zhan Jifeng stated that, according to his lawyer's investigation with the Education Bureau, the registered editor of the newspaper was not Zhang Yuyan, but Li Muzhi, so Zhang was actually a substitute, and Li should be summoned to the case. Zhang Yuyan stated that he had been the editor since the tenth issue, and Li had been the editor before the tenth issue. As for the point in the manuscript that the plaintiff had a relationship with Xu Qinfu, there were rumors of this outside, and this newspaper was to refute the rumors. Judge Ge stated that June 20th was the first issue of the "Camera" tabloid, so Li must be summoned to the case. He then ordered the case to be postponed to the 13th of this month for further hearing and summoned Li Muzhi and the "Camera" tabloid to the case for investigation.

Pu Xiyuan Comes to Shanghai

▲ Displaying Calligraphy and Paintings at Youzheng Bookstore

Pu Tong, a famous member of the Qing imperial family, is skilled in calligraphy, painting, and songwriting, and his name is highly respected. He is currently a professor at Tsinghua University and has come to Shanghai for sightseeing during the summer vacation. He has written and painted various Buddhist pagodas, including the Heart Sutra, Amitayus Sutra, Amitabha Sutra, and Universal Gate Chapter, using inner court magnetic blue paper, real gold, and solemn Buddhist images. The fonts are free and elegant, and the decorations are exquisite. They are on display at the Youzheng Bookstore for public viewing.

Bao He Tang Holds Charitable Free Clinic

The Hongkou Branch of Bao He Tang on North Sichuan Road is holding a charitable free clinic for the purpose of relieving the poor and sick. Several national doctors have been specially hired to provide free clinics at the bureau from 7:00 am to 5:00 pm every day, without charging any fees.
